# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

Handles exact matches, suffix wildcards, and prefix wildcards.\\n- `findWildcardVirtualHost()` method: Implements wildcard matching algorithm for virtual hosts, supporting longest wildcard match patterns (e.g., \\\"*-bar.baz.com\\\" matches before \\\"*.baz.com\\\").\\n- The RouteMatcher maintains data structures: `virtual_hosts_` (hash map for exact matches), `wildcard_virtual_host_suffixes_` and `wildcard_virtual_host_prefixes_` (maps for wildcard patterns sorted by specificity).\\n\\n## Route Matching Algorithm\\nThe route matching logic is implemented in `CommonVirtualHostImpl` and `VirtualHostImpl` classes in `source/common/router/config_impl.h` and `config_impl.cc`. matching in Envoy is implemented across several C++ source files in the envoyproxy/envoy repository (version v1.31.2). The implementation is split into three main components:\\n\\n## Virtual Host Selection\\nThe `RouteMatcher` class in `source/common/router/config_impl.h` and `config_impl.cc` handles virtual host selection. It provides:\\n- `findVirtualHost()` method: Performs host/domain matching against request headers to select the appropriate virtual host. Handles exact matches, suffix wildcards, and prefix wildcards.\\n- `findWildcardVirtualHost()` method: Implements wildcard matching algorithm for virtual hosts, supporting longest wildcard match patterns (e.g., \\\"*-bar.baz.com\\\" matches before \\\"*.baz.com\\\").\\n- The RouteMatcher maintains data structures: `virtual_hosts_` (hash map for exact matches), `wildcard_virtual_host_suffixes_` and `wildcard_virtual_host_prefixes_` (maps for wildcard patterns sorted by specificity).\\n\\n## Route Matching Algorithm\\nThe route matching logic is implemented in `CommonVirtualHostImpl` and `VirtualHostImpl` classes in `source/common/router/config_impl.h` and `config_impl.cc`. Key components include:\\n- `VirtualHostImpl::getRouteFromEntries()`: Iterates through configured routes and calls `matches()` on each route entry to find the first matching route.\\n- `VirtualHostImpl::getRouteFromRoutes()`: Similar pattern for route lists, processes routes in order.\\n- Multiple route entry implementation classes handle different path matching patterns:\\n  - `PrefixRouteEntryImpl`: Matches request paths by prefix\\n  - `PathRouteEntryImpl`: Matches exact request paths\\n  - `RegexRouteEntryImpl`: Matches paths using regular expressions\\n  - `UriTemplateMatcherRouteEntryImpl`: Matches paths using URI template patterns\\n  - `ConnectRouteEntryImpl`: Matches CONNECT requests\\n  - `PathSeparatedPrefixRouteEntryImpl`: Matches path-separated prefix patterns\\n- Each route entry class implements `matches()` method from the `Matchable` interface to evaluate request headers against the route's match criteria.\\n- Route matching also considers additional criteria: header matching, query parameters, runtime features, TLS context, and gRPC options.\\n\\n## Route Action Dispatch\\nThe router filter in `source/common/router/router.h` and `router.cc` orchestrates the routing decision:\\n- `Filter::decodeHeaders()` method (line 431 in router.cc): Main entry point that receives incoming request headers. It calls `callbacks_->route()` to trigger route matching.\\n- The filter first checks for a matching route (line 454), handling the \\\"no route found\\\" case.\\n- Then it checks for direct responses (line 466) which may generate local responses without contacting upstream clusters.\\n- Finally, it extracts the route entry (line 492) and proceeds with the actual route action dispatch.\\n- `RouteMatchAction` and `RouteListMatchAction` classes encapsulate actions to be taken when routes match in the matching tree.\\n- The `FilterConfig` class provides configuration and factory context for the filter.\\n\\n## Configuration and Integration\\nThe HTTP connection manager configuration is handled in `source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h` and `config.cc`, which integrates the router configuration provider and route matching through the `RouteMatcher` instance managed by `CommonConfigImpl`.\\n\\nThe route matching flow chain: HTTP Request \u2192 RouteMatcher::findVirtualHost() (virtual host selection) \u2192 VirtualHostImpl::getRouteFromEntries() (route iteration) \u2192 RouteEntry::matches() (path/header matching) \u2192 Route Action Dispatch in Filter::decodeHeaders().\"\n}\n",
